# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/Chip/

On this page

# Chip

Chips are compact elements that can represent inputs, attributes, or actions.
They can have an icon or avatar on the left, and a close button icon on the right.
They are typically used to:

* Present multiple options
* Represent attributes active or chosen
* Present filter options
* Trigger actions related to primary content

* flat
* outlined

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/chip-1.png)

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/chip-2.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { Chip } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => (  
  <Chip icon="information" onPress={() => console.log('Pressed')}>Example Chip</Chip>  
);  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### mode[​](#mode "Direct link to mode")

Type: `'flat' | 'outlined'`

Default value: `'flat'`

Mode of the chip.

* `flat` - flat chip without outline.
* `outlined` - chip with an outline.

### children (required)[​](#children-required "Direct link to children (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Text content of the `Chip`.

### icon[​](#icon "Direct link to icon")

Type: [`IconSource`](https://github.com/callstack/react-native-paper/blob/main/src/components/Icon.tsx#L16)

Icon to display for the `Chip`. Both icon and avatar cannot be specified.

### avatar[​](#avatar "Direct link to avatar")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Avatar to display for the `Chip`. Both icon and avatar cannot be specified.

### closeIcon[​](#closeicon "Direct link to closeIcon")

Type: [`IconSource`](https://github.com/callstack/react-native-paper/blob/main/src/components/Icon.tsx#L16)

Icon to display as the close button for the `Chip`. The icon appears only when the onClose prop is specified.

### selected[​](#selected "Direct link to selected")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Whether chip is selected.

### selectedColor[​](#selectedcolor "Direct link to selectedColor")

Type: `string`

Whether to style the chip color as selected.
Note: With theme version 3 `selectedColor` doesn't apply to the `icon`.
If you want specify custom color for the `icon`, render your own `Icon` component.

### showSelectedOverlay Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#showselectedoverlay--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to showselectedoverlay--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Whether to display overlay on selected chip

### showSelectedCheck[​](#showselectedcheck "Direct link to showSelectedCheck")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `true`

Whether to display default check icon on selected chip.
Note: Check will not be shown if `icon` is specified. If specified, `icon` will be shown regardless of `selected`.

### rippleColor[​](#ripplecolor "Direct link to rippleColor")

Type: `ColorValue`

Color of the ripple effect.

### disabled[​](#disabled "Direct link to disabled")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Whether the chip is disabled. A disabled chip is greyed out and `onPress` is not called on touch.

### background[​](#background "Direct link to background")

Type: `PressableAndroidRippleConfig`

Type of background drawabale to display the feedback (Android).
<https://reactnative.dev/docs/pressable#rippleconfig>

### accessibilityLabel[​](#accessibilitylabel "Direct link to accessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

Accessibility label for the chip. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the chip.

### closeIconAccessibilityLabel[​](#closeiconaccessibilitylabel "Direct link to closeIconAccessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

Default value: `'Close'`

Accessibility label for the close icon. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the close icon.

### onPress[​](#onpress "Direct link to onPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on press.

### onLongPress[​](#onlongpress "Direct link to onLongPress")

Type: `() => void`

Function to execute on long press.

### onPressIn[​](#onpressin "Direct link to onPressIn")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute as soon as the touchable element is pressed and invoked even before onPress.

### onPressOut[​](#onpressout "Direct link to onPressOut")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute as soon as the touch is released even before onPress.

### onClose[​](#onclose "Direct link to onClose")

Type: `() => void`

Function to execute on close button press. The close button appears only when this prop is specified.

### delayLongPress[​](#delaylongpress "Direct link to delayLongPress")

Type: `number`

The number of milliseconds a user must touch the element before executing `onLongPress`.

### compact Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#compact--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to compact--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `boolean`

Sets smaller horizontal paddings `12dp` around label, when there is only label.

### elevated Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#elevated--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to elevated--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Whether chip should have the elevation.

### textStyle[​](#textstyle "Direct link to textStyle")

Type: [`StyleProp<TextStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/text-style-props)

Style of chip's text

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: `Animated.WithAnimatedValue<StyleProp<ViewStyle>>`

### hitSlop[​](#hitslop "Direct link to hitSlop")

Type: `TouchableRippleProps['hitSlop']`

Sets additional distance outside of element in which a press can be detected.

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### testID[​](#testid "Direct link to testID")

Type: `string`

Default value: `'chip'`

Pass down testID from chip props to touchable for Detox tests.

### ellipsizeMode[​](#ellipsizemode "Direct link to ellipsizeMode")

Type: `EllipsizeProp`

Ellipsize Mode for the children text

### maxFontSizeMultiplier[​](#maxfontsizemultiplier "Direct link to maxFontSizeMultiplier")

Type: `number`

Specifies the largest possible scale a text font can reach.

### accessibilityRole[​](#accessibilityrole "Direct link to accessibilityRole")

Type:

Default value: `'button'`

# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/DataTable/

On this page

# DataTable

Data tables allow displaying sets of data.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/data-table-full-width.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { DataTable } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => {  
  const [page, setPage] = React.useState<number>(0);  
  const [numberOfItemsPerPageList] = React.useState([2, 3, 4]);  
  const [itemsPerPage, onItemsPerPageChange] = React.useState(  
    numberOfItemsPerPageList[0]  
  );  
  
  const [items] = React.useState([  
   {  
     key: 1,  
     name: 'Cupcake',  
     calories: 356,  
     fat: 16,  
   },  
   {  
     key: 2,  
     name: 'Eclair',  
     calories: 262,  
     fat: 16,  
   },  
   {  
     key: 3,  
     name: 'Frozen yogurt',  
     calories: 159,  
     fat: 6,  
   },  
   {  
     key: 4,  
     name: 'Gingerbread',  
     calories: 305,  
     fat: 3.7,  
   },  
  ]);  
  
  const from = page * itemsPerPage;  
  const to = Math.min((page + 1) * itemsPerPage, items.length);  
  
  React.useEffect(() => {  
    setPage(0);  
  }, [itemsPerPage]);  
  
  return (  
    <DataTable>  
      <DataTable.Header>  
        <DataTable.Title>Dessert</DataTable.Title>  
        <DataTable.Title numeric>Calories</DataTable.Title>  
        <DataTable.Title numeric>Fat</DataTable.Title>  
      </DataTable.Header>  
  
      {items.slice(from, to).map((item) => (  
        <DataTable.Row key={item.key}>  
          <DataTable.Cell>{item.name}</DataTable.Cell>  
          <DataTable.Cell numeric>{item.calories}</DataTable.Cell>  
          <DataTable.Cell numeric>{item.fat}</DataTable.Cell>  
        </DataTable.Row>  
      ))}  
  
      <DataTable.Pagination  
        page={page}  
        numberOfPages={Math.ceil(items.length / itemsPerPage)}  
        onPageChange={(page) => setPage(page)}  
        label={`${from + 1}-${to} of ${items.length}`}  
        numberOfItemsPerPageList={numberOfItemsPerPageList}  
        numberOfItemsPerPage={itemsPerPage}  
        onItemsPerPageChange={onItemsPerPageChange}  
        showFastPaginationControls  
        selectPageDropdownLabel={'Rows per page'}  
      />  
    </DataTable>  
  );  
};  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### children (required)[​](#children-required "Direct link to children (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Content of the `DataTable`.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/DataTable/DataTablePagination

On this page

# DataTable.Pagination

A component to show pagination for data table.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/data-table-pagination.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { DataTable } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const numberOfItemsPerPageList = [2, 3, 4];  
  
const items = [  
  {  
    key: 1,  
    name: 'Page 1',  
  },  
  {  
    key: 2,  
    name: 'Page 2',  
  },  
  {  
    key: 3,  
    name: 'Page 3',  
  },  
];  
  
const MyComponent = () => {  
  const [page, setPage] = React.useState(0);  
  const [numberOfItemsPerPage, onItemsPerPageChange] = React.useState(numberOfItemsPerPageList[0]);  
  const from = page * numberOfItemsPerPage;  
  const to = Math.min((page + 1) * numberOfItemsPerPage, items.length);  
  
  React.useEffect(() => {  
     setPage(0);  
  }, [numberOfItemsPerPage]);  
  
  return (  
    <DataTable>  
      <DataTable.Pagination  
        page={page}  
        numberOfPages={Math.ceil(items.length / numberOfItemsPerPage)}  
        onPageChange={page => setPage(page)}  
        label={`${from + 1}-${to} of ${items.length}`}  
        showFastPaginationControls  
        numberOfItemsPerPageList={numberOfItemsPerPageList}  
        numberOfItemsPerPage={numberOfItemsPerPage}  
        onItemsPerPageChange={onItemsPerPageChange}  
        selectPageDropdownLabel={'Rows per page'}  
      />  
    </DataTable>  
  );  
};  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### page (required)[​](#page-required "Direct link to page (required)")

Type: `number`

The currently visible page (starting with 0).

### numberOfPages (required)[​](#numberofpages-required "Direct link to numberOfPages (required)")

Type: `number`

The total number of pages.

### onPageChange (required)[​](#onpagechange-required "Direct link to onPageChange (required)")

Type: `(page: number) => void`

Function to execute on page change.

### showFastPaginationControls[​](#showfastpaginationcontrols "Direct link to showFastPaginationControls")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Whether to show fast forward and fast rewind buttons in pagination. False by default.

### paginationControlRippleColor[​](#paginationcontrolripplecolor "Direct link to paginationControlRippleColor")

Type: `ColorValue`

Color of the pagination control ripple effect.

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### numberOfItemsPerPage[​](#numberofitemsperpage "Direct link to numberOfItemsPerPage")

Type: `number`

The current number of rows per page.

### numberOfItemsPerPageList[​](#numberofitemsperpagelist "Direct link to numberOfItemsPerPageList")

Type: `Array<number>`

Options for a number of rows per page to choose from.

### onItemsPerPageChange[​](#onitemsperpagechange "Direct link to onItemsPerPageChange")

Type: `(numberOfItemsPerPage: number) => void`

The function to set the number of rows per page.

### dropdownItemRippleColor[​](#dropdownitemripplecolor "Direct link to dropdownItemRippleColor")

Type: `ColorValue`

Color of the dropdown item ripple effect.

### selectPageDropdownRippleColor[​](#selectpagedropdownripplecolor "Direct link to selectPageDropdownRippleColor")

Type: `ColorValue`

Color of the select page dropdown ripple effect.

### selectPageDropdownLabel[​](#selectpagedropdownlabel "Direct link to selectPageDropdownLabel")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Label text for select page dropdown to display.

### selectPageDropdownAccessibilityLabel[​](#selectpagedropdownaccessibilitylabel "Direct link to selectPageDropdownAccessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

AccessibilityLabel for `selectPageDropdownLabel`.

### label[​](#label "Direct link to label")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Label text to display which indicates current pagination.

### accessibilityLabel[​](#accessibilitylabel "Direct link to accessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

AccessibilityLabel for `label`.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

* [Props](#props)
  + [page (required)](#page-required)
  + [numberOfPages (required)](#numberofpages-required)
  + [onPageChange (required)](#onpagechange-required)
  + [showFastPaginationControls](#showfastpaginationcontrols)
  + [paginationControlRippleColor](#paginationcontrolripplecolor)

# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/Dialog/

On this page

# Dialog

Dialogs inform users about a specific task and may contain critical information, require decisions, or involve multiple tasks.
To render the `Dialog` above other components, you'll need to wrap it with the [`Portal`](/react-native-paper/docs/Portal) component.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/dialog-1.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { View } from 'react-native';  
import { Button, Dialog, Portal, PaperProvider, Text } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => {  
  const [visible, setVisible] = React.useState(false);  
  
  const showDialog = () => setVisible(true);  
  
  const hideDialog = () => setVisible(false);  
  
  return (  
    <PaperProvider>  
      <View>  
        <Button onPress={showDialog}>Show Dialog</Button>  
        <Portal>  
          <Dialog visible={visible} onDismiss={hideDialog}>  
            <Dialog.Title>Alert</Dialog.Title>  
            <Dialog.Content>  
              <Text variant="bodyMedium">This is simple dialog</Text>  
            </Dialog.Content>  
            <Dialog.Actions>  
              <Button onPress={hideDialog}>Done</Button>  
            </Dialog.Actions>  
          </Dialog>  
        </Portal>  
      </View>  
    </PaperProvider>  
  );  
};  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### dismissable[​](#dismissable "Direct link to dismissable")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `true`

Determines whether clicking outside the dialog dismiss it.

### dismissableBackButton[​](#dismissablebackbutton "Direct link to dismissableBackButton")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `dismissable`

Determines whether clicking Android hardware back button dismiss dialog.

### onDismiss[​](#ondismiss "Direct link to onDismiss")

Type: `() => void`

Callback that is called when the user dismisses the dialog.

### visible[​](#visible "Direct link to visible")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Determines Whether the dialog is visible.

### children (required)[​](#children-required "Direct link to children (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Content of the `Dialog`.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: `Animated.WithAnimatedValue<StyleProp<ViewStyle>>`

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### testID[​](#testid "Direct link to testID")

Type: `string`

testID to be used on tests.

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

| mode | backgroundColor |
| --- | --- |
| - | theme.colors.elevation.level3 |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<Dialog theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`

* [Usage](#usage)
* [Props](#props)
  + [dismissable](#dismissable)
  + [dismissableBackButton](#dismissablebackbutton)
  + [onDismiss](#ondismiss)
  + [visible](#visible)
  + [children (required)](#children-required)
  + [style](#style)
  + [theme](#theme)
  + [testID](#testid)
* [Theme colors](#theme-colors)

# Dialog.Actions

A component to show a list of actions in a Dialog.

```

  return (  
    <Portal>  
      <Dialog visible={visible} onDismiss={hideDialog}>  
        <Dialog.Actions>  
          <Button onPress={() => console.log('Cancel')}>Cancel</Button>  
          <Button onPress={() => console.log('Ok')}>Ok</Button>  
        </Dialog.Actions>  
      </Dialog>  
    </Portal>  
  );
```

# Dialog.Icon

@supported Available in v5.x with theme version 3
A component to show an icon in a Dialog.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/dialog-icon.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { StyleSheet } from 'react-native';  
import { Dialog, Portal, Text } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => {  
  const [visible, setVisible] = React.useState(false);  
  
  const hideDialog = () => setVisible(false);  
  
  return (  
    <Portal>  
      <Dialog visible={visible} onDismiss={hideDialog}>  
        <Dialog.Icon icon="alert" />  
        <Dialog.Title style={styles.title}>This is a title</Dialog.Title>  
        <Dialog.Content>  
          <Text variant="bodyMedium">This is simple dialog</Text>  
        </Dialog.Content>  
      </Dialog>  
    </Portal>  
  );  
};  
  
const styles = StyleSheet.create({  
  title: {  
    textAlign: 'center',  
  },  
})  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### color[​](#color "Direct link to color")

Type: `string`

Custom color for action icon.

### icon (required)[​](#icon-required "Direct link to icon (required)")

Type: [`IconSource`](https://github.com/callstack/react-native-paper/blob/main/src/components/Icon.tsx#L16)

Name of the icon to show.

### size[​](#size "Direct link to size")

Type: `number`

Default value: `24`

Optional icon size.

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

| mode | iconColor |
| --- | --- |
| - | theme.colors.secondary |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<Dialog.Icon theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`

# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/Dialog/DialogScrollArea

# Dialog.ScrollArea

A component to show a scrollable content in a Dialog. The component only provides appropriate styling.
For the scrollable content you can use `ScrollView`, `FlatList` etc. depending on your requirement.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/dialog-scroll-area.gif)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { ScrollView } from 'react-native';  
import { Dialog, Portal, Text } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => {  
  const [visible, setVisible] = React.useState(false);  
  
  const hideDialog = () => setVisible(false);  
  
  return (  
    <Portal>  
      <Dialog visible={visible} onDismiss={hideDialog}>  
        <Dialog.ScrollArea>  
          <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={{paddingHorizontal: 24}}>  
            <Text>This is a scrollable area</Text>  
          </ScrollView>  
        </Dialog.ScrollArea>  
      </Dialog>  
    </Portal>  
  );  
};  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### children (required)[​](#children-required "Direct link to children (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Content of the `DialogScrollArea`.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

| mode | borderColor |
| --- | --- |
| - | theme.colors.surfaceVariant |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<Dialog.ScrollArea theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`

# Divider

A divider is a thin, lightweight separator that groups content in lists and page layouts.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/divider.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { View } from 'react-native';  
import { Divider, Text } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => (  
  <View>  
    <Text>Lemon</Text>  
    <Divider />  
    <Text>Mango</Text>  
    <Divider />  
  </View>  
);  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### leftInset Renamed from 'inset' to 'leftInset` in v5.x[​](#leftinset--renamed-from-inset-to-leftinset-in-v5x "Direct link to leftinset--renamed-from-inset-to-leftinset-in-v5x")

Type: `boolean`

Whether divider has a left inset.

### horizontalInset Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#horizontalinset--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to horizontalinset--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Whether divider has a horizontal inset on both sides.

### bold Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#bold--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to bold--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Whether divider should be bolded.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

| mode | dividerColor |
| --- | --- |
| - | theme.colors.outlineVariant |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<Divider theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`

# Drawer.CollapsedItem

Note: Available in v5.x with theme version 3

Collapsed component used to show an action item with an icon and optionally label in a navigation drawer.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/drawer-collapsed.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { Drawer } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => (  
   <Drawer.CollapsedItem  
     focusedIcon="inbox"  
     unfocusedIcon="inbox-outline"  
     label="Inbox"  
   />  
);  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### label[​](#label "Direct link to label")

Type: `string`

The label text of the item.

### badge[​](#badge "Direct link to badge")

Type: `string | number | boolean`

Default value: `false`

Badge to show on the icon, can be `true` to show a dot, `string` or `number` to show text.

### disabled[​](#disabled "Direct link to disabled")

Type: `boolean`

Whether the item is disabled.

### focusedIcon Renamed from 'icon' to 'focusedIcon' in v5.x[​](#focusedicon--renamed-from-icon-to-focusedicon-in-v5x "Direct link to focusedicon--renamed-from-icon-to-focusedicon-in-v5x")

Type: [`IconSource`](https://github.com/callstack/react-native-paper/blob/main/src/components/Icon.tsx#L16)

Icon to use as the focused destination icon, can be a string, an image source or a react component

### unfocusedIcon Renamed from 'icon' to 'focusedIcon' in v5.x[​](#unfocusedicon--renamed-from-icon-to-focusedicon-in-v5x "Direct link to unfocusedicon--renamed-from-icon-to-focusedicon-in-v5x")

Type: [`IconSource`](https://github.com/callstack/react-native-paper/blob/main/src/components/Icon.tsx#L16)

Icon to use as the unfocused destination icon, can be a string, an image source or a react component

### active[​](#active "Direct link to active")

Type: `boolean`

Whether to highlight the drawer item as active.

### onPress[​](#onpress "Direct link to onPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on press.

### labelMaxFontSizeMultiplier[​](#labelmaxfontsizemultiplier "Direct link to labelMaxFontSizeMultiplier")

Type: `number`

Specifies the largest possible scale a label font can reach.

### accessibilityLabel[​](#accessibilitylabel "Direct link to accessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

Accessibility label for the button. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the button.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### testID[​](#testid "Direct link to testID")

Type: `string`

Default value: `'drawer-collapsed-item'`

TestID used for testing purposes

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

| mode | backgroundColor | textColor | iconColor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| active | theme.colors.secondaryContainer | theme.colors.onSurface | theme.colors.onSecondaryContainer |
| inactive |  | theme.colors.onSurfaceVariant | theme.colors.onSurfaceVariant |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<Drawer.CollapsedItem theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`

# Drawer.Section

A component to group content inside a navigation drawer.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/drawer-section.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { Drawer } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => {  
  const [active, setActive] = React.useState('');  
  
  return (  
    <Drawer.Section title="Some title">  
      <Drawer.Item  
        label="First Item"  
        active={active === 'first'}  
        onPress={() => setActive('first')}  
      />  
      <Drawer.Item  
        label="Second Item"  
        active={active === 'second'}  
        onPress={() => setActive('second')}  
      />  
    </Drawer.Section>  
  );  
};  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### title[​](#title "Direct link to title")

Type: `string`

Title to show as the header for the section.

### children (required)[​](#children-required "Direct link to children (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Content of the `Drawer.Section`.

### showDivider[​](#showdivider "Direct link to showDivider")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `true`

Whether to show `Divider` at the end of the section. True by default.

### titleMaxFontSizeMultiplier[​](#titlemaxfontsizemultiplier "Direct link to titleMaxFontSizeMultiplier")

Type: `number`

Specifies the largest possible scale a title font can reach.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

| mode | titleColor |
| --- | --- |
| - | theme.colors.onSurfaceVariant |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<Drawer.Section theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`

# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/FAB/

On this page

# FAB

A floating action button represents the primary action on a screen. It appears in front of all screen content.

* all variants
* all sizes
* all modes
* with label

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/fab-1.png)

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/fab-2.png)

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/fab-4.png)

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/fab-3.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { StyleSheet } from 'react-native';  
import { FAB } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => (  
  <FAB  
    icon="plus"  
    style={styles.fab}  
    onPress={() => console.log('Pressed')}  
  />  
);  
  
const styles = StyleSheet.create({  
  fab: {  
    position: 'absolute',  
    margin: 16,  
    right: 0,  
    bottom: 0,  
  },  
})  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### icon[​](#icon "Direct link to icon")

Type: [`IconSource`](https://github.com/callstack/react-native-paper/blob/main/src/components/Icon.tsx#L16)

Icon to display for the `FAB`. It's optional only if `label` is defined.

### label[​](#label "Direct link to label")

Type: `string`

Optional label for extended `FAB`. It's optional only if `icon` is defined.

### uppercase[​](#uppercase "Direct link to uppercase")

Type: `boolean`

Make the label text uppercased.

### background[​](#background "Direct link to background")

Type: `PressableAndroidRippleConfig`

Type of background drawabale to display the feedback (Android).
<https://reactnative.dev/docs/pressable#rippleconfig>

### accessibilityLabel[​](#accessibilitylabel "Direct link to accessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

Default value: `label`

Accessibility label for the FAB. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the FAB.
Uses `label` by default if specified.

### accessibilityState[​](#accessibilitystate "Direct link to accessibilityState")

Type: [`AccessibilityState`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/accessibility#accessibilitystate)

Accessibility state for the FAB. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the FAB.

### animated[​](#animated "Direct link to animated")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `true`

Whether an icon change is animated.

### small Deprecated in v.5x - use prop size="small".[​](#small--deprecated-in-v5x---use-prop-sizesmall "Direct link to small--deprecated-in-v5x---use-prop-sizesmall")

Type: `boolean`

Whether FAB is mini-sized, used to create visual continuity with other elements. This has no effect if `label` is specified.

### color[​](#color "Direct link to color")

Type: `string`

Custom color for the icon and label of the `FAB`.

### rippleColor[​](#ripplecolor "Direct link to rippleColor")

Type: `ColorValue`

Color of the ripple effect.

### disabled[​](#disabled "Direct link to disabled")

Type: `boolean`

Whether `FAB` is disabled. A disabled button is greyed out and `onPress` is not called on touch.

### visible[​](#visible "Direct link to visible")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `true`

Whether `FAB` is currently visible.

### loading[​](#loading "Direct link to loading")

Type: `boolean`

Whether to show a loading indicator.

### onPress[​](#onpress "Direct link to onPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on press.

### onLongPress[​](#onlongpress "Direct link to onLongPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on long press.

### delayLongPress[​](#delaylongpress "Direct link to delayLongPress")

Type: `number`

The number of milliseconds a user must touch the element before executing `onLongPress`.

### size Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#size--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to size--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `'small' | 'medium' | 'large'`

Default value: `'medium'`

Size of the `FAB`.

* `small` - FAB with small height (40).
* `medium` - FAB with default medium height (56).
* `large` - FAB with large height (96).

### customSize[​](#customsize "Direct link to customSize")

Type: `number`

Custom size for the `FAB`. This prop takes precedence over size prop

### mode Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#mode--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to mode--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `'flat' | 'elevated'`

Default value: `'elevated'`

Mode of the `FAB`. You can change the mode to adjust the the shadow:

* `flat` - button without a shadow.
* `elevated` - button with a shadow.

### variant Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#variant--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to variant--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `'primary' | 'secondary' | 'tertiary' | 'surface'`

Default value: `'primary'`

Color mappings variant for combinations of container and icon colors.

### labelMaxFontSizeMultiplier[​](#labelmaxfontsizemultiplier "Direct link to labelMaxFontSizeMultiplier")

Type: `number`

Specifies the largest possible scale a label font can reach.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: `Animated.WithAnimatedValue<StyleProp<ViewStyle>>`

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### testID[​](#testid "Direct link to testID")

Type: `string`

Default value: `'fab'`

TestID used for testing purposes

### ref[​](#ref "Direct link to ref")

Type: `React.RefObject<View>`

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

| mode | backgroundColor | textColor/iconColor |
| --- | --- | --- |
| disabled | theme.colors.surfaceDisabled | theme.colors.onSurfaceDisabled |
| primary | theme.colors.primaryContainer | theme.colors.onPrimaryContainer |
| secondary | theme.colors.secondaryContainer | theme.colors.onSecondaryContainer |
| tertiary | theme.colors.tertiaryContainer | theme.colors.onTertiaryContainer |
| surface | theme.colors.elevarion.level3 | theme.colors.primary |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<FAB theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`

# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/FAB/AnimatedFAB

On this page

# AnimatedFAB

An animated, extending horizontally floating action button represents the primary action in an application.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/animated-fab.gif)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import React from 'react';  
import {  
  StyleProp,  
  ViewStyle,  
  Animated,  
  StyleSheet,  
  Platform,  
  ScrollView,  
  Text,  
  SafeAreaView,  
  I18nManager,  
} from 'react-native';  
import { AnimatedFAB } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = ({  
  animatedValue,  
  visible,  
  extended,  
  label,  
  animateFrom,  
  style,  
  iconMode,  
}) => {  
  const [isExtended, setIsExtended] = React.useState(true);  
  
  const isIOS = Platform.OS === 'ios';  
  
  const onScroll = ({ nativeEvent }) => {  
    const currentScrollPosition =  
      Math.floor(nativeEvent?.contentOffset?.y) ?? 0;  
  
    setIsExtended(currentScrollPosition <= 0);  
  };  
  
  const fabStyle = { [animateFrom]: 16 };  
  
  return (  
    <SafeAreaView style={styles.container}>  
      <ScrollView onScroll={onScroll}>  
        {[...new Array(100).keys()].map((_, i) => (  
          <Text>{i}</Text>  
        ))}  
      </ScrollView>  
      <AnimatedFAB  
        icon={'plus'}  
        label={'Label'}  
        extended={isExtended}  
        onPress={() => console.log('Pressed')}  
        visible={visible}  
        animateFrom={'right'}  
        iconMode={'static'}  
        style={[styles.fabStyle, style, fabStyle]}  
      />  
    </SafeAreaView>  
  );  
};  
  
export default MyComponent;  
  
const styles = StyleSheet.create({  
  container: {  
    flexGrow: 1,  
  },  
  fabStyle: {  
    bottom: 16,  
    right: 16,  
    position: 'absolute',  
  },  
});
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### icon (required)[​](#icon-required "Direct link to icon (required)")

Type: [`IconSource`](https://github.com/callstack/react-native-paper/blob/main/src/components/Icon.tsx#L16)

Icon to display for the `FAB`.

### label (required)[​](#label-required "Direct link to label (required)")

Type: `string`

Label for extended `FAB`.

### uppercase[​](#uppercase "Direct link to uppercase")

Type: `boolean`

Make the label text uppercased.

### background[​](#background "Direct link to background")

Type: `PressableAndroidRippleConfig`

Type of background drawabale to display the feedback (Android).
<https://reactnative.dev/docs/pressable#rippleconfig>

### accessibilityLabel[​](#accessibilitylabel "Direct link to accessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

Default value: `label`

Accessibility label for the FAB. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the FAB.
Uses `label` by default if specified.

### accessibilityState[​](#accessibilitystate "Direct link to accessibilityState")

Type: [`AccessibilityState`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/accessibility#accessibilitystate)

Accessibility state for the FAB. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the FAB.

### color[​](#color "Direct link to color")

Type: `string`

Custom color for the icon and label of the `FAB`.

### rippleColor[​](#ripplecolor "Direct link to rippleColor")

Type: `ColorValue`

Color of the ripple effect.

### disabled[​](#disabled "Direct link to disabled")

Type: `boolean`

Whether `FAB` is disabled. A disabled button is greyed out and `onPress` is not called on touch.

### visible[​](#visible "Direct link to visible")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `true`

Whether `FAB` is currently visible.

### onPress[​](#onpress "Direct link to onPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on press.

### onLongPress[​](#onlongpress "Direct link to onLongPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on long press.

### delayLongPress[​](#delaylongpress "Direct link to delayLongPress")

Type: `number`

The number of milliseconds a user must touch the element before executing `onLongPress`.

### iconMode[​](#iconmode "Direct link to iconMode")

Type: `'static' | 'dynamic'`

Default value: `'dynamic'`

Whether icon should be translated to the end of extended `FAB` or be static and stay in the same place. The default value is `dynamic`.

### animateFrom[​](#animatefrom "Direct link to animateFrom")

Type: `'left' | 'right'`

Default value: `'right'`

Indicates from which direction animation should be performed. The default value is `right`.

### extended[​](#extended "Direct link to extended")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Whether `FAB` should start animation to extend.

### labelMaxFontSizeMultiplier[​](#labelmaxfontsizemultiplier "Direct link to labelMaxFontSizeMultiplier")

Type: `number`

Specifies the largest possible scale a label font can reach.

### variant Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#variant--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to variant--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `'primary' | 'secondary' | 'tertiary' | 'surface'`

Default value: `'primary'`

Color mappings variant for combinations of container and icon colors.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: `Animated.WithAnimatedValue<StyleProp<ViewStyle>>`

### hitSlop[​](#hitslop "Direct link to hitSlop")

Type: `TouchableRippleProps['hitSlop']`

Sets additional distance outside of element in which a press can be detected.

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### testID[​](#testid "Direct link to testID")

Type: `string`

Default value: `'animated-fab'`

TestID used for testing purposes

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

| mode | backgroundColor | textColor/iconColor |
| --- | --- | --- |
| disabled | theme.colors.surfaceDisabled | theme.colors.onSurfaceDisabled |
| primary | theme.colors.primaryContainer | theme.colors.onPrimaryContainer |
| secondary | theme.colors.secondaryContainer | theme.colors.onSecondaryContainer |
| tertiary | theme.colors.tertiaryContainer | theme.colors.onTertiaryContainer |
| surface | theme.colors.elevarion.level3 | theme.colors.primary |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<AnimatedFAB theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`

# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/FAB/FABGroup

# FAB.Group

A component to display a stack of FABs with related actions in a speed dial.
To render the group above other components, you'll need to wrap it with the [`Portal`](/react-native-paper/docs/components/Portal) component.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/fab-group.gif)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { FAB, Portal, PaperProvider } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => {  
  const [state, setState] = React.useState({ open: false });  
  
  const onStateChange = ({ open }) => setState({ open });  
  
  const { open } = state;  
  
  return (  
    <PaperProvider>  
      <Portal>  
        <FAB.Group  
          open={open}  
          visible  
          icon={open ? 'calendar-today' : 'plus'}  
          actions={[  
            { icon: 'plus', onPress: () => console.log('Pressed add') },  
            {  
              icon: 'star',  
              label: 'Star',  
              onPress: () => console.log('Pressed star'),  
            },  
            {  
              icon: 'email',  
              label: 'Email',  
              onPress: () => console.log('Pressed email'),  
            },  
            {  
              icon: 'bell',  
              label: 'Remind',  
              onPress: () => console.log('Pressed notifications'),  
            },  
          ]}  
          onStateChange={onStateChange}  
          onPress={() => {  
            if (open) {  
              // do something if the speed dial is open  
            }  
          }}  
        />  
      </Portal>  
    </PaperProvider>  
  );  
};  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### actions (required)[​](#actions-required "Direct link to actions (required)")

Type: `Array<{
icon: IconSource;
label?: string;
color?: string;
labelTextColor?: string;
accessibilityLabel?: string;
accessibilityHint?: string;
style?: Animated.WithAnimatedValue<StyleProp<ViewStyle>>;
containerStyle?: Animated.WithAnimatedValue<StyleProp<ViewStyle>>;
wrapperStyle?: StyleProp<ViewStyle>;
labelStyle?: StyleProp<TextStyle>;
labelMaxFontSizeMultiplier?: number;
onPress: (e: GestureResponderEvent) => void;
size?: 'small' | 'medium';
testID?: string;
rippleColor?: ColorValue;
}>`

Action items to display in the form of a speed dial.
An action item should contain the following properties:

* `icon`: icon to display (required)
* `label`: optional label text
* `color`: custom icon color of the action item
* `labelTextColor`: custom label text color of the action item
* `accessibilityLabel`: accessibility label for the action, uses label by default if specified
* `accessibilityHint`: accessibility hint for the action
* `style`: pass additional styles for the fab item, for example, `backgroundColor`
* `containerStyle`: pass additional styles for the fab item label container, for example, `backgroundColor` Available in 5.x
* `wrapperStyle`: pass additional styles for the wrapper of the action item.
* `labelStyle`: pass additional styles for the fab item label, for example, `fontSize`
* `labelMaxFontSizeMultiplier`: specifies the largest possible scale a title font can reach.
* `onPress`: callback that is called when `FAB` is pressed (required)
* `onLongPress`: callback that is called when `FAB` is long pressed
* `toggleStackOnLongPress`: callback that is called when `FAB` is long pressed
* `size`: size of action item. Defaults to `small`. Available in v5.x
* `testID`: testID to be used on tests
* `rippleColor`: color of the ripple effect.

### icon (required)[​](#icon-required "Direct link to icon (required)")

Type: [`IconSource`](https://github.com/callstack/react-native-paper/blob/main/src/components/Icon.tsx#L16)

Icon to display for the `FAB`.
You can toggle it based on whether the speed dial is open to display a different icon.

### accessibilityLabel[​](#accessibilitylabel "Direct link to accessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

Accessibility label for the FAB. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the FAB.

### color[​](#color "Direct link to color")

Type: `string`

Custom color for the `FAB`.

### backdropColor[​](#backdropcolor "Direct link to backdropColor")

Type: `string`

Custom backdrop color for opened speed dial background.

### rippleColor[​](#ripplecolor "Direct link to rippleColor")

Type: `ColorValue`

Color of the ripple effect.

### onPress[​](#onpress "Direct link to onPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on pressing the `FAB`.

### onLongPress[​](#onlongpress "Direct link to onLongPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on long pressing the `FAB`.

### toggleStackOnLongPress[​](#togglestackonlongpress "Direct link to toggleStackOnLongPress")

Type: `boolean`

Makes actions stack appear on long press instead of on press.

### delayLongPress[​](#delaylongpress "Direct link to delayLongPress")

Type: `number`

Default value: `200`

Changes the delay for long press reaction.

### enableLongPressWhenStackOpened[​](#enablelongpresswhenstackopened "Direct link to enableLongPressWhenStackOpened")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Allows for onLongPress when stack is opened.

### open (required)[​](#open-required "Direct link to open (required)")

Type: `boolean`

Whether the speed dial is open.

### onStateChange (required)[​](#onstatechange-required "Direct link to onStateChange (required)")

Type: `(state: { open: boolean }) => void`

Callback which is called on opening and closing the speed dial.
The open state needs to be updated when it's called, otherwise the change is dropped.

### visible (required)[​](#visible-required "Direct link to visible (required)")

Type: `boolean`

Whether `FAB` is currently visible.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

Style for the group. You can use it to pass additional styles if you need.
For example, you can set an additional padding if you have a tab bar at the bottom.

### fabStyle[​](#fabstyle "Direct link to fabStyle")

Type: `Animated.WithAnimatedValue<StyleProp<ViewStyle>>`

Style for the FAB. It allows to pass the FAB button styles, such as backgroundColor.

### variant Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#variant--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to variant--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `'primary' | 'secondary' | 'tertiary' | 'surface'`

Default value: `'primary'`

Color mappings variant for combinations of container and icon colors.

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### label[​](#label "Direct link to label")

Type: `string`

Optional label for `FAB`.

### testID[​](#testid "Direct link to testID")

Type: `string`

Pass down testID from Group props to FAB.

# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/HelperText/

On this page

# HelperText

Helper text is used in conjuction with input elements to provide additional hints for the user.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/helper-text.gif)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { View } from 'react-native';  
import { HelperText, TextInput } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => {  
  const [text, setText] = React.useState('');  
  
   const onChangeText = text => setText(text);  
  
  const hasErrors = () => {  
    return !text.includes('@');  
  };  
  
 return (  
    <View>  
      <TextInput label="Email" value={text} onChangeText={onChangeText} />  
      <HelperText type="error" visible={hasErrors()}>  
        Email address is invalid!  
      </HelperText>  
    </View>  
  );  
};  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### type[​](#type "Direct link to type")

Type: `'error' | 'info'`

Default value: `'info'`

Type of the helper text.

### children (required)[​](#children-required "Direct link to children (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Text content of the HelperText.

### visible[​](#visible "Direct link to visible")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `true`

Whether to display the helper text.

### padding[​](#padding "Direct link to padding")

Type: `'none' | 'normal'`

Default value: `'normal'`

Whether to apply padding to the helper text.

### disabled[​](#disabled "Direct link to disabled")

Type: `boolean`

Whether the text input tied with helper text is disabled.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: [`StyleProp<TextStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/text-style-props)

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### testID[​](#testid "Direct link to testID")

Type: `string`

TestID used for testing purposes

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

| mode | textColor |
| --- | --- |
| disabled | theme.colors.onSurfaceDisabled |
| default | theme.colors.onSurfaceVariant |
| error | theme.colors.error |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<HelperText theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`

# IconButton

An icon button is a button which displays only an icon without a label.

* default
* outlined
* contained
* contained-tonal

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/icon-button-1.png)

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/icon-button-4.png)

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/icon-button-2.png)

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/icon-button-3.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { IconButton, MD3Colors } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => (  
  <IconButton  
    icon="camera"  
    iconColor={MD3Colors.error50}  
    size={20}  
    onPress={() => console.log('Pressed')}  
  />  
);  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### TouchableRipple props[​](#touchableripple-props "Direct link to TouchableRipple props")

*Extends:* [`...TouchableRipple props`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/TouchableRipple)

### icon (required)[​](#icon-required "Direct link to icon (required)")

Type: [`IconSource`](https://github.com/callstack/react-native-paper/blob/main/src/components/Icon.tsx#L16)

Icon to display.

### mode Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#mode--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to mode--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `'outlined' | 'contained' | 'contained-tonal'`

Mode of the icon button. By default there is no specified mode - only pressable icon will be rendered.

### iconColor Renamed from 'color' to 'iconColor' in v5.x[​](#iconcolor--renamed-from-color-to-iconcolor-in-v5x "Direct link to iconcolor--renamed-from-color-to-iconcolor-in-v5x")

Type: `string`

Color of the icon.

### containerColor[​](#containercolor "Direct link to containerColor")

Type: `string`

Background color of the icon container.

### rippleColor[​](#ripplecolor "Direct link to rippleColor")

Type: `ColorValue`

Color of the ripple effect.

### selected Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#selected--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to selected--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Whether icon button is selected. A selected button receives alternative combination of icon and container colors.

### size[​](#size "Direct link to size")

Type: `number`

Default value: `24`

Size of the icon.

### disabled[​](#disabled "Direct link to disabled")

Type: `boolean`

Whether the button is disabled. A disabled button is greyed out and `onPress` is not called on touch.

### animated[​](#animated "Direct link to animated")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Whether an icon change is animated.

### accessibilityLabel[​](#accessibilitylabel "Direct link to accessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

Accessibility label for the button. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the button.

### contentStyle[​](#contentstyle "Direct link to contentStyle")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

Style of button's inner content.
Use this prop to apply custom height and width or to set a custom padding`.

### onPress[​](#onpress "Direct link to onPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on press.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: `Animated.WithAnimatedValue<StyleProp<ViewStyle>>`

### ref[​](#ref "Direct link to ref")

Type: `React.RefObject<View>`

### testID[​](#testid "Direct link to testID")

Type: `string`

Default value: `'icon-button'`

TestID used for testing purposes

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### loading[​](#loading "Direct link to loading")

Type: `boolean`

Default value: `false`

Whether to show a loading indicator.

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

* selected
* unselected
* disabled

| mode | iconColor | backgroundColor | borderColor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| default | theme.colors.primary |  |  |
| outlined | theme.colors.inverseOnSurface | theme.colors.inverseSurface |  |
| contained | theme.colors.onPrimary | theme.colors.primary |  |
| contained-tonal | theme.colors.onSecondaryContainer | theme.colors.secondaryContainer |  |

| mode | iconColor | backgroundColor | borderColor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| default | theme.colors.onSurfaceVariant |  |  |
| outlined | theme.colors.onSurfaceVariant |  | theme.colors.outline |
| contained | theme.colors.primary | theme.colors.surfaceVariant |  |
| contained-tonal | theme.colors.onSurfaceVariant | theme.colors.surfaceVariant |  |

| mode | iconColor | backgroundColor | borderColor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| default | theme.colors.onSurfaceDisabled |  |  |
| outlined | theme.colors.onSurfaceDisabled | theme.colors.surfaceDisabled | theme.colors.surfaceDisabled |
| contained | theme.colors.onSurfaceDisabled | theme.colors.surfaceDisabled |  |
| contained-tonal | theme.colors.onSurfaceDisabled | theme.colors.surfaceDisabled |  |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<IconButton theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`

# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/List/ListAccordion

On this page

# List.Accordion

A component used to display an expandable list item.

* with left icon
* with description
* items with icon

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/list-accordion-1.png)

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/list-accordion-2.png)

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/list-accordion-3.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { List } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => {  
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = React.useState(true);  
  
  const handlePress = () => setExpanded(!expanded);  
  
  return (  
    <List.Section title="Accordions">  
      <List.Accordion  
        title="Uncontrolled Accordion"  
        left={props => <List.Icon {...props} icon="folder" />}>  
        <List.Item title="First item" />  
        <List.Item title="Second item" />  
      </List.Accordion>  
  
      <List.Accordion  
        title="Controlled Accordion"  
        left={props => <List.Icon {...props} icon="folder" />}  
        expanded={expanded}  
        onPress={handlePress}>  
        <List.Item title="First item" />  
        <List.Item title="Second item" />  
      </List.Accordion>  
    </List.Section>  
  );  
};  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### title (required)[​](#title-required "Direct link to title (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Title text for the list accordion.

### description[​](#description "Direct link to description")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Description text for the list accordion.

### left[​](#left "Direct link to left")

Type: `(props: { color: string; style: Style }) => React.ReactNode`

Callback which returns a React element to display on the left side.

### right[​](#right "Direct link to right")

Type: `(props: { isExpanded: boolean }) => React.ReactNode`

Callback which returns a React element to display on the right side.

### expanded[​](#expanded "Direct link to expanded")

Type: `boolean`

Whether the accordion is expanded
If this prop is provided, the accordion will behave as a "controlled component".
You'll need to update this prop when you want to toggle the component or on `onPress`.

### onPress[​](#onpress "Direct link to onPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on press.

### onLongPress[​](#onlongpress "Direct link to onLongPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on long press.

### delayLongPress[​](#delaylongpress "Direct link to delayLongPress")

Type: `number`

The number of milliseconds a user must touch the element before executing `onLongPress`.

### children (required)[​](#children-required "Direct link to children (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Content of the section.

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### background[​](#background "Direct link to background")

Type: `PressableAndroidRippleConfig`

Type of background drawabale to display the feedback (Android).
<https://reactnative.dev/docs/pressable#rippleconfig>

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

Style that is passed to the root TouchableRipple container.

### containerStyle[​](#containerstyle "Direct link to containerStyle")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

Style that is passed to the outermost container that wraps the entire content, including left and right items and both title and description.

### contentStyle[​](#contentstyle "Direct link to contentStyle")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

Style that is passed to the content container, which wraps the title and description.

### titleStyle[​](#titlestyle "Direct link to titleStyle")

Type: [`StyleProp<TextStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/text-style-props)

Style that is passed to Title element.

### descriptionStyle[​](#descriptionstyle "Direct link to descriptionStyle")

Type: [`StyleProp<TextStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/text-style-props)

Style that is passed to Description element.

### rippleColor[​](#ripplecolor "Direct link to rippleColor")

Type: `ColorValue`

Color of the ripple effect.

### titleNumberOfLines[​](#titlenumberoflines "Direct link to titleNumberOfLines")

Type: `number`

Default value: `1`

Truncate Title text such that the total number of lines does not
exceed this number.

### descriptionNumberOfLines[​](#descriptionnumberoflines "Direct link to descriptionNumberOfLines")

Type: `number`

Default value: `2`

Truncate Description text such that the total number of lines does not
exceed this number.

### titleMaxFontSizeMultiplier[​](#titlemaxfontsizemultiplier "Direct link to titleMaxFontSizeMultiplier")

Type: `number`

Specifies the largest possible scale a title font can reach.

### descriptionMaxFontSizeMultiplier[​](#descriptionmaxfontsizemultiplier "Direct link to descriptionMaxFontSizeMultiplier")

Type: `number`

Specifies the largest possible scale a description font can reach.

### id[​](#id "Direct link to id")

Type: `string | number`

Id is used for distinguishing specific accordion when using List.AccordionGroup. Property is required when using List.AccordionGroup and has no impact on behavior when using standalone List.Accordion.

### testID[​](#testid "Direct link to testID")

Type: `string`

TestID used for testing purposes

### accessibilityLabel[​](#accessibilitylabel "Direct link to accessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

Accessibility label for the TouchableRipple. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the touchable.

### pointerEvents[​](#pointerevents "Direct link to pointerEvents")

Type: `ViewProps['pointerEvents']`

Default value: `'none'`

`pointerEvents` passed to the `View` container

### hitSlop[​](#hitslop "Direct link to hitSlop")

Type: `TouchableRippleProps['hitSlop']`

Amount of space between the touchable area and the edge of the component.
This can be used to enlarge the touchable area beyond the visible component.

# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/List/ListAccordionGroup

On this page

# List.AccordionGroup

List.AccordionGroup allows to control a group of List Accordions. `id` prop for List.Accordion is required in order for group to work.
List.AccordionGroup can be a controlled or uncontrolled component. The example shows the uncontrolled version.
At most one Accordion can be expanded at a given time.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/list-accordion-group.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { View, Text } from 'react-native';  
import { List } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => (  
  <List.AccordionGroup>  
    <List.Accordion title="Accordion 1" id="1">  
      <List.Item title="Item 1" />  
    </List.Accordion>  
    <List.Accordion title="Accordion 2" id="2">  
      <List.Item title="Item 2" />  
    </List.Accordion>  
    <View>  
      <Text>  
        List.Accordion can be wrapped because implementation uses React.Context.  
      </Text>  
      <List.Accordion title="Accordion 3" id="3">  
        <List.Item title="Item 3" />  
      </List.Accordion>  
    </View>  
  </List.AccordionGroup>  
);  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### onAccordionPress[​](#onaccordionpress "Direct link to onAccordionPress")

Type: `(expandedId: string | number) => void`

Function to execute on selection change.

### expandedId[​](#expandedid "Direct link to expandedId")

Type: `string | number`

Id of the currently expanded list accordion

### children (required)[​](#children-required "Direct link to children (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

React elements containing list accordions

* [Usage](#usage)
* [Props](#props)
  + [onAccordionPress](#onaccordionpress)
  + [expandedId](#expandedid)
  + [children (required)](#children-required)

# Page: https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/components/Menu/

On this page

# Menu

Menus display a list of choices on temporary elevated surfaces. Their placement varies based on the element that opens them.

* with icons
* without icons

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/menu-1.png)

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/menu-2.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { View } from 'react-native';  
import { Button, Menu, Divider, PaperProvider } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => {  
  const [visible, setVisible] = React.useState(false);  
  
  const openMenu = () => setVisible(true);  
  
  const closeMenu = () => setVisible(false);  
  
  return (  
    <PaperProvider>  
      <View  
        style={{  
          paddingTop: 50,  
          flexDirection: 'row',  
          justifyContent: 'center',  
        }}>  
        <Menu  
          visible={visible}  
          onDismiss={closeMenu}  
          anchor={<Button onPress={openMenu}>Show menu</Button>}>  
          <Menu.Item onPress={() => {}} title="Item 1" />  
          <Menu.Item onPress={() => {}} title="Item 2" />  
          <Divider />  
          <Menu.Item onPress={() => {}} title="Item 3" />  
        </Menu>  
      </View>  
    </PaperProvider>  
  );  
};  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

### Note[​](#note "Direct link to Note")

When using `Menu` within a React Native's `Modal` component, you need to wrap all
`Modal` contents within a `PaperProvider` in order for the menu to show. This
wrapping is not necessary if you use Paper's `Modal` instead.

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### visible (required)[​](#visible-required "Direct link to visible (required)")

Type: `boolean`

Whether the Menu is currently visible.

### anchor (required)[​](#anchor-required "Direct link to anchor (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode | { x: number; y: number }`

The anchor to open the menu from. In most cases, it will be a button that opens the menu.

### anchorPosition[​](#anchorposition "Direct link to anchorPosition")

Type: `'top' | 'bottom'`

Whether the menu should open at the top of the anchor or at its bottom.
Applied only when anchor is a node, not an x/y position.

### statusBarHeight[​](#statusbarheight "Direct link to statusBarHeight")

Type: `number`

Extra margin to add at the top of the menu to account for translucent status bar on Android.
If you are using Expo, we assume translucent status bar and set a height for status bar automatically.
Pass `0` or a custom value to and customize it.
This is automatically handled on iOS.

### onDismiss[​](#ondismiss "Direct link to onDismiss")

Type: `() => void`

Callback called when Menu is dismissed. The `visible` prop needs to be updated when this is called.

### overlayAccessibilityLabel[​](#overlayaccessibilitylabel "Direct link to overlayAccessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

Default value: `'Close menu'`

Accessibility label for the overlay. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps outside the menu.

### children (required)[​](#children-required "Direct link to children (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Content of the `Menu`.

### contentStyle[​](#contentstyle "Direct link to contentStyle")

Type: `Animated.WithAnimatedValue<StyleProp<ViewStyle>>`

Style of menu's inner content.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

### elevation[​](#elevation "Direct link to elevation")

Type: `MD3Elevation`

Default value: `2`

Elevation level of the menu's content. Shadow styles are calculated based on this value. Default `backgroundColor` is taken from the corresponding `theme.colors.elevation` property. By default equals `2`.
Available in v5.x with theme version 3

### mode[​](#mode "Direct link to mode")

Type: `'flat' | 'elevated'`

Default value: `'elevated'`

Mode of the menu's content.

* `elevated` - Surface with a shadow and background color corresponding to set `elevation` value.
* `flat` - Surface without a shadow, with the background color corresponding to set `elevation` value.

Available in v5.x with theme version 3

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### keyboardShouldPersistTaps[​](#keyboardshouldpersisttaps "Direct link to keyboardShouldPersistTaps")

Type: `ScrollViewProps['keyboardShouldPersistTaps']`

Inner ScrollView prop

### testID[​](#testid "Direct link to testID")

Type: `string`

Default value: `'menu'`

testID to be used on tests.

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

| mode | backgroundColor |
| --- | --- |
| - | theme.colors.elevation.level2 |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<Menu theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`

  + [onDismiss](#ondismiss)
  + [overlayAccessibilityLabel](#overlayaccessibilitylabel)

# Menu.Item

A component to show a single list item inside a Menu.

![](/react-native-paper/screenshots/menu-item.png)

## Usage[​](#usage "Direct link to Usage")

```
import * as React from 'react';  
import { View } from 'react-native';  
import { Menu } from 'react-native-paper';  
  
const MyComponent = () => (  
  <View style={{ flex: 1 }}>  
    <Menu.Item leadingIcon="redo" onPress={() => {}} title="Redo" />  
    <Menu.Item leadingIcon="undo" onPress={() => {}} title="Undo" />  
    <Menu.Item leadingIcon="content-cut" onPress={() => {}} title="Cut" disabled />  
    <Menu.Item leadingIcon="content-copy" onPress={() => {}} title="Copy" disabled />  
    <Menu.Item leadingIcon="content-paste" onPress={() => {}} title="Paste" />  
  </View>  
);  
  
export default MyComponent;
```

## Props[​](#props "Direct link to Props")

### title (required)[​](#title-required "Direct link to title (required)")

Type: `React.ReactNode`

Title text for the `MenuItem`.

### leadingIcon Renamed from 'icon' to 'leadingIcon' in v5.x[​](#leadingicon--renamed-from-icon-to-leadingicon-in-v5x "Direct link to leadingicon--renamed-from-icon-to-leadingicon-in-v5x")

Type: [`IconSource`](https://github.com/callstack/react-native-paper/blob/main/src/components/Icon.tsx#L16)

Leading icon to display for the `MenuItem`.

### trailingIcon Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#trailingicon--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to trailingicon--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: [`IconSource`](https://github.com/callstack/react-native-paper/blob/main/src/components/Icon.tsx#L16)

Trailing icon to display for the `MenuItem`.

### disabled[​](#disabled "Direct link to disabled")

Type: `boolean`

Whether the 'item' is disabled. A disabled 'item' is greyed out and `onPress` is not called on touch.

### dense Available in v5.x with theme version 3[​](#dense--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3 "Direct link to dense--available-in-v5x-with-theme-version-3")

Type: `boolean`

Sets min height with densed layout.

### background[​](#background "Direct link to background")

Type: `PressableAndroidRippleConfig`

Type of background drawabale to display the feedback (Android).
<https://reactnative.dev/docs/pressable#rippleconfig>

### onPress[​](#onpress "Direct link to onPress")

Type: `(e: GestureResponderEvent) => void`

Function to execute on press.

### titleMaxFontSizeMultiplier[​](#titlemaxfontsizemultiplier "Direct link to titleMaxFontSizeMultiplier")

Type: `number`

Default value: `1.5`

Specifies the largest possible scale a title font can reach.

### style[​](#style "Direct link to style")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

Style that is passed to the root TouchableRipple container.

### containerStyle[​](#containerstyle "Direct link to containerStyle")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

Style that is passed to the outermost container that wraps the entire content, including leading and trailing icons and title text.

### contentStyle[​](#contentstyle "Direct link to contentStyle")

Type: [`StyleProp<ViewStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/view-style-props)

Style that is passed to the content container, which wraps the title text.

### titleStyle[​](#titlestyle "Direct link to titleStyle")

Type: [`StyleProp<TextStyle>`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/text-style-props)

Style that is passed to the Title element.

### rippleColor[​](#ripplecolor "Direct link to rippleColor")

Type: `ColorValue`

Color of the ripple effect.

### theme[​](#theme "Direct link to theme")

Type: [`ThemeProp`](https://callstack.github.io/react-native-paper/docs/guides/theming#theme-properties)

### hitSlop[​](#hitslop "Direct link to hitSlop")

Type: `TouchableRippleProps['hitSlop']`

Sets additional distance outside of element in which a press can be detected.

### testID[​](#testid "Direct link to testID")

Type: `string`

Default value: `'menu-item'`

TestID used for testing purposes

### accessibilityLabel[​](#accessibilitylabel "Direct link to accessibilityLabel")

Type: `string`

Accessibility label for the Touchable. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the component.

### accessibilityState[​](#accessibilitystate "Direct link to accessibilityState")

Type: [`AccessibilityState`](https://reactnative.dev/docs/accessibility#accessibilitystate)

Accessibility state for the Touchable. This is read by the screen reader when the user taps the component.

## Theme colors[​](#theme-colors "Direct link to Theme colors")

info

The table below outlines the theme colors, specifically for MD3 *(theme version 3)* at the moment.

| mode | textColor | iconColor |
| --- | --- | --- |
| default | theme.colors.onSurface | theme.colors.onSurfaceVariant |
| disabled | theme.colors.onSurfaceDisabled | theme.colors.onSurfaceDisabled |

tip

If a dedicated prop for a specific color is not available or the `style` prop does not allow color modification, you can customize it using the `theme` prop. It allows to override any color, within the component, based on the table above.

*Example of overriding* `primary` *color:*

`<Menu.Item theme={{ colors: { primary: 'green' } }} />`
